### ✓ 2026-05-10: Cross-review topics/forward-in-time-conscious-selection.md considering decision-void.md insights
- **Type**: cross-review
- **Notes**: Chain from today's 2026-05-10 expand-topic of `voids/decision-void.md`. The new article names decision-void as positioned at "the most theoretically motivated site for non-physical influence on the physical world" and lists `[[forward-in-time-conscious-selection]]` as one of its primary topics — yet `obsidian/topics/forward-in-time-conscious-selection.md` does not currently link to decision-void (verified 2026-05-10). The relationship is structurally important: forward-in-time-conscious-selection treats the post-decoherence selection mechanism at branch points; decision-void treats the phenomenology of the same moment from the inside. Cross-review should (a) install a substantive bridging clause where forward-in-time-conscious-selection treats the conscious-selection moment, naming decision-void as the inside-view companion to the outside-view mechanism; (b) verify that the article's three-mechanisms taxonomy (Stapp Process 1/Process 3, von Neumann cut, decoherence-timescale selection) is consistent with decision-void's discrimination problem (the void's three faces apply differently to each mechanism); (c) check whether the article's empirical-considerations list (~lines 158–170) needs to acknowledge that the conscious-selection moment's phenomenological inaccessibility is structurally predicted by decision-void's argument; (d) reciprocate links and `related_articles`. Short-medium scope (~200–300 words touched). Tenet alignment: Tenet 2 (Minimal Quantum Interaction) + Tenet 3 (Bidirectional Interaction) + methodological.
- **Output**: obsidian/topics/forward-in-time-conscious-selection.md -- Context: Cross-review topics/forward-in-time-conscious-selection.md considering decision-void.md insights

### ✓ 2026-05-10: Refine voids/decision-void.md to fix label leakage and overstatements
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: Pessimistic review on 2026-05-10 (see [pessimistic-2026-05-10b](/reviews/pessimistic-2026-05-10b/)) found three structural issues that the catalogue's outer-review consensus has flagged elsewhere as the primary structural weakness. **Critical**: §"Deflationary Alternatives" uses editor-vocabulary "Mode One / Mode Two / Mode Three" labels in prose (lines 90, 92, 94) and invokes [direct-refutation-discipline](/project/direct-refutation-discipline/) as a hyperlinked authority-citation introducing a classification scheme — exactly the label-leakage failure mode. The fix: remove the labels and engage each opposing position substantively. Wegner illusionism in particular needs engagement of *The Illusion of Conscious Will* chapters 4–5 rather than the "Mode Two — unsupported foundational move" classification dismissal — Wegner *did* give a positive account of robustness/cross-cultural-similarity. **Critical**: three citations of [evidential-status-discipline](/project/evidential-status-discipline/) (lines 68, 96, 122) function as authority-appeal where the qualifying language should be in the prose directly. **Medium-high**: Soon et al. (2008) "predicted the specific outcome" reads as deterministic — the actual classifier accuracy was ~60% on a binary 50/50 task; the article's own evidential-status concerns require the magnitude be reported. **High**: the abductive-evidence-for-dualism claim (line 104) rests on the strawman "physicalism predicts these should converge with sufficient introspective skill" — most physicalists (Dennett, Churchland) actively predict persistent asymmetry; either drop the strawman or cite a specific physicalist who makes the convergence prediction. **Medium**: the three-face independence claim is asserted not argued; add a paragraph showing each face could in principle vary independently. **Medium**: "most theoretically motivated" comparative claim (lines 50, 100, 122) is uncited; downgrade to "primary candidate site" or argue the comparison. Quantum-mechanism citations (Stapp, Penrose-Hameroff) need decoherence-objection acknowledgement or removal. Strengths to preserve: conjunction-coalesce structure, sibling-distinctions section, reflexivity acknowledgement, site-perspective integration.
- **Output**: obsidian/voids/decision-void.md

### ✓ 2026-05-10: Write voids article on the Decision Void
- **Type**: expand-topic
- **Notes**: Unconsumed research from `research/voids-decision-void-2026-05-10.md` (today's research). The Decision Void names the structural opacity at the deliberation→commitment crossing — the *snap* moment when open weighing collapses into sealed choice. The research distinguishes it sharply from agency-void (voluntariness/downstream causation), noetic-feelings-void (audited feelings of knowing/rightness), and transit-void (crossings generally). Unique among voids: positioned at the most plausible candidate locus for any non-physical influence on the physical world, where MQI's empirical grip is sharpest. Empirical anchors: Libet (1983), Soon-Brass-Heinze-Haynes (2008) 7-second predictability, Johansson-Hall choice blindness (2005); phenomenological backbone: Pacherie (2008), Mele (2009), Ricoeur on the categorical finality of the act of deciding. The article should (a) name the void cleanly (the *moment* of commitment, not the deliberation that precedes or the action that follows); (b) marshal the three empirical anchors at calibrated weight — Libet's readiness-potential debate is contested (Schurger et al. 2012 stochastic-accumulation reading), Soon's 7-second figure is real but the predictive information is configural rather than deterministic; (c) honour [evidential-status-discipline](/project/evidential-status-discipline/) — the empirical findings *constrain but do not establish* where the decision happens; the gap leaves room for either fully-physical-with-conscious-registration or non-physical-commitment-with-physical-precipitation, and the Map's MQI tenet gives the latter reading without claiming the data forces it; (d) install the Pacherie/Mele/Ricoeur phenomenology as evidence that the act has a categorical, non-decomposable structure — itself a sign the constitutive act resists internal articulation; (e) deploy [direct-refutation-discipline](/project/direct-refutation-discipline/) for the deflationary alternatives (Soon-style fully-physical reading is Mode Three; Wegner-style illusionism about the decision-experience is Mode Two); (f) connect to [forward-in-time-conscious-selection](/topics/forward-in-time-conscious-selection/) as the Map's positive mechanism candidate; (g) install reciprocal links across the four sibling voids the research distinguishes from. **Capacity**: voids/ at 99/100 = essentially capped — this consumes the last slot. The decision is justified by tenet-load-bearing uniqueness (no other void targets MQI as directly) and by empirical anchorage (other unconsumed void research notes — translation, effort, recurrence — are more interpretive, less empirically forced). Estimated scope: 2000–2800 words. Tenet alignment: Tenet 2 (Minimal Quantum Interaction) load-bearing — the void at the most natural empirical interface; Tenet 3 (Bidirectional Interaction). See research file.
- **Output**: Write voids article on the Decision Void

### ✓ 2026-05-10: Add discrimination-problem section to topics/phenomenology-of-memory-and-the-self.md
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: Singleton P2 from `reviews/outer-review-synthesis-2026-05-10.md` (Claude Opus 4.7 finding) that was missed during synthesis-to-todo task installation today — the synthesis explicitly listed it (line 87) but the corresponding entry never landed in the queue. The target article uses "pastness quale" terminology 7× without ever explaining how the felt-as-past discriminates *memory* from *imagining* or *hallucinating*. Without this, the pastness quale is underspecified — any vivid mental image accompanied by a strong feeling of "this happened" would qualify, which is precisely what produces confabulation and source-monitoring errors. Bernecker (2010 *Memory*), Michaelian (2016 *Mental Time Travel*), McCarroll (2018 *Remembering from the Outside*), and Robins (2016) converge on the importance of this discrimination problem. Refine should add a new section ("Discrimination problem" or similar) that (a) names the problem — pastness alone is insufficient unless it discriminates memory from same-content imagination/hallucination; (b) engages McCarroll's observer-vs-field memory work and Robins's process-vs-product distinction; (c) cites Bernecker on memory's success conditions and Michaelian on simulationism's reply (memory as imagination of the past, with no need for a discriminating quale); (d) states what the Map's framework requires — either a *content* of pastness that discriminates structurally, or a separate *source-monitoring* mechanism that the phenomenology accurately reflects, or honest acknowledgement that the discrimination problem is partially open; (e) bridges to the Klein & Nichols pathology argument and the AD/MCI counterevidence section that landed today. Apply [direct-refutation-discipline](/project/direct-refutation-discipline/) and [evidential-status-discipline](/project/evidential-status-discipline/) — the Map should not paper over a known underspecification when the literature has named it. Estimated scope: ~300–500 words added. Tenet alignment: Tenet 4 (No Many Worlds) load-bearing through the pastness-quale → personal-identity inference; methodological / [evidential-status-discipline](/project/evidential-status-discipline/) / [direct-refutation-discipline](/project/direct-refutation-discipline/). Sequencing: independent of the three completed P1 refines from today's synthesis cycle; safe to execute alongside the singleton P2 atemporal-causation cross-review. See `reviews/outer-review-2026-05-10-claude-opus-4-7.md` line 193 (Improvement 1d) and synthesis line 87.
- **Output**: obsidian/topics/phenomenology-of-memory-and-the-self.md

### ✓ 2026-05-10: Add discrimination-problem section to topics/phenomenology-of-memory-and-the-self.md
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: Singleton P2 from `reviews/outer-review-synthesis-2026-05-10.md` (Claude Opus 4.7 finding). The target article used "pastness quale" terminology 7× without explaining how the felt-as-past discriminates memory from imagining or hallucinating. Added new section "The Discrimination Problem" (~520 words) between "Pastness: phenomenal property or metacognitive/simulationist feeling?" and "The Pastness Quale and Irreducibility". Engages Bernecker (2010) on memory's success conditions, McCarroll (2018) on observer-vs-field memories, Robins (2016) on the process-vs-product distinction, and Michaelian (2016) on simulationism's reply. States the Map's three available positions (structural pastness content; reflective source-monitoring with accurate phenomenology; partially open) and bridges to the Klein–Nichols mineness dissociation and AD/MCI semantic-continuity sections added earlier today. Updated transition phrase in the deflationary-engagements section ("staged next" → "staged below in the irreducibility section"). Added 3 references (Bernecker 2010, McCarroll 2018, Robins 2016 — last two flagged for human verification). Engagement modes: Bernecker / McCarroll / Robins all Mode One concession; Michaelian mixed Mode One + Mode Three (simulationism's internal consistency conceded; the strong reductive conclusion declined at the framework boundary).
- **Output**: obsidian/topics/phenomenology-of-memory-and-the-self.md

### ✓ 2026-05-10: Apply new dissociation-levels rule from evidential-status-discipline across dissociation-using articles
- **Type**: cross-review
- **Notes**: Chain from today's 2026-05-10 refine of `obsidian/project/evidential-status-discipline.md`. The rule: *Dissociation arguments must separate four levels — separability (the two phenomena come apart in the data); phenomenological reality (one is a genuine feature of experience); mechanistic independence (different processes underlie them); metaphysical irreducibility (the dissociated feature cannot be physically/functionally explained). Evidence for one level should not automatically be counted as evidence for the next.* Cross-review pass should: (a) identify articles using clinical or anomaly dissociations as load-bearing evidence — Klein & Nichols (2012) patient KC, Capgras, blindsight, alien-hand, Anton's syndrome, Anosognosia, Naccache et al. (2005) effortless-control ACC-lesion, Würzburg–Titchener cognitive-phenomenology dissociation, Tippett/Prebble & Addis (2018) AD/MCI, the just-completed apex/phenomenal-output-causal-machinery-dissociation.md cluster, etc.; (b) for each, verify the article distinguishes the four levels rather than sliding from separability to metaphysical irreducibility; (c) install hedging where the article over-claims; (d) flag articles where the four-level audit reveals load-bearing slides for follow-up refine. The just-completed mineness-inference refine of `topics/phenomenology-of-memory-and-the-self.md` (2026-05-10) is the worked-example template — use that as the pattern for what the audit looks like in practice. Short-medium scope (~400–700 words touched across 5–10 files). Prioritise files that the apex/phenomenal-output-causal-machinery-dissociation cluster cites as source articles (these are the most-load-bearing dissociation-using articles in the catalogue). Tenet alignment: methodological / [evidential-status-discipline](/project/evidential-status-discipline/) / [direct-refutation-discipline](/project/direct-refutation-discipline/). See [evidential-status-discipline](/project/evidential-status-discipline/) (post-2026-05-10 refine).
- **Output**: obsidian/project/evidential-status-discipline.md -- Context: Apply new dissociation-levels rule from evidential-status-discipline across dissociation-using articles

### ✓ 2026-05-10: Apply new MWI-checklist rule from evidential-status-discipline across MWI-touching articles
- **Type**: cross-review
- **Notes**: Chain from today's 2026-05-10 refine of `obsidian/project/evidential-status-discipline.md` (commit landed; the discipline now includes a "MWI-specific review checklist" rule). The rule: *Before any article claims to refute MWI, require it to answer: "Could an Everettian restate this phenomenon as branch-local, centered, and determinate?" If yes, classify the disagreement as a framework boundary (Mode Three in [direct-refutation-discipline](/project/direct-refutation-discipline/) terms) unless there is an additional argument for why global ontological uniqueness is required by the phenomenon.* The rule operationalises the boundary-substitution failure mode that five independent outer reviewers have now converged on (2026-05-03 ChatGPT, 2026-05-04 ChatGPT, 2026-05-04 Claude, 2026-05-10 ChatGPT and Claude). Cross-review pass should: (a) grep for MWI / many-worlds / Many-Worlds / Everett across `topics/`, `concepts/`, `apex/`, and `arguments/` (~140+ candidate files; prioritise the load-bearing ones — `arguments/many-worlds-argument.md`, `topics/quantum-holism-and-phenomenal-unity.md`, `topics/phenomenology-of-memory-and-the-self.md`, `topics/consciousness-and-probability-interpretation.md`, and any apex articles invoking MWI rejection); (b) for each load-bearing claim that *refutes* MWI, verify the article either passes the checklist or explicitly classifies the disagreement as framework-boundary; (c) install the checklist invocation as a methodological reference where the article's claim survives but should be hedged as Mode Three; (d) flag any article where the checklist reveals an unrecoverable refutation claim for follow-up refine. Short-medium scope (~300–600 words touched across 4–8 files). Tenet alignment: Tenet 4 (No Many Worlds) + methodological. See [evidential-status-discipline](/project/evidential-status-discipline/) (post-2026-05-10 refine) and [direct-refutation-discipline](/project/direct-refutation-discipline/).
- **Output**: obsidian/project/evidential-status-discipline.md -- Context: Apply new MWI-checklist rule from evidential-status-discipline across MWI-touching articles

### ✓ 2026-05-10: Refine topics/phenomenology-of-memory-and-the-self.md with AD/MCI semantic-continuity counterevidence
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: From outer review by Claude Opus 4.7 2026-05-10. The article's autonoetic-primacy thesis — phenomenological continuity (autonoetic re-experiencing carrying mineness) underwrites diachronic identity — is directly challenged by Tippett, Prebble & Addis (2018) and Klein (2012, 2014) on AD/MCI: diachronic unity can be supported by *semantic* continuity when phenomenological continuity is degraded. This is a published empirical result the article does not engage. The refine must either (a) argue that semantic continuity is an *inadequate* substitute for diachronic identity (not by recapitulating the autonoetic-primacy thesis but by an independent argument), or (b) weaken the autonoetic-primacy claim to "one route among others." The KC presentation in the article (line 81) treats KC as showing clean episodic-vs-semantic dissociation; Rosenbaum et al. (2005) and Tulving's later analyses indicate residual semantic-autobiographical structure that complicates the clean dissociation. Update the KC paragraph to acknowledge that nuance while preserving the article's central point about the phenomenological distinctness of episodic re-experiencing. ~250–400 words touched. Tenet alignment: empirical hedging / [evidential-status-discipline](/project/evidential-status-discipline/). See review file.
- **Output**: obsidian/topics/phenomenology-of-memory-and-the-self.md

### ✓ 2026-05-10: Cross-review concepts/atemporal-causation.md against topics/phenomenology-of-memory-and-the-self.md to resolve the retrocausal-vs-pastness paradox
- **Type**: cross-review
- **Notes**: From outer review by Gemini 2.5 Pro 2026-05-10. **Genuinely new finding** (not flagged by ChatGPT or Claude in this cycle). The Map endorses atemporal-causation / TSVF / transactional-QM machinery in `concepts/atemporal-causation.md` (the page exists; the reviewer's claim is verified) — and uses this to support Minimal Quantum Interaction by allowing conscious decisions to influence neural precursors via backward-in-time handshakes. But the topic article on memory simultaneously commits to the pastness quale as an "encounter with objective past" (Husserlian linear-time framing). If retrocausal influence is admitted, the past is not a fixed objective reality being encountered but a fluid construct being retroactively shaped — destabilizing the pastness quale's load-bearing role in the Map's anti-MWI argument. Cross-review should: (a) read both articles in the light of each other; (b) state the apparent tension explicitly in the appropriate article (likely a paragraph in `topics/phenomenology-of-memory-and-the-self.md` and a reciprocal note in `concepts/atemporal-causation.md`); (c) attempt a unified position — perhaps that retrocausality operates only at the quantum-interface layer and does not propagate into the macroscopic phenomenological encounter, OR explicitly mark this as a [direct-refutation-discipline](/project/direct-refutation-discipline/) Mode Three boundary disagreement; (d) update wikilinks for navigability. ~300–500 words touched across both files. Tenet alignment: Tenet 2 (Minimal Quantum Interaction) ↔ Tenet 4 (No Many Worlds); methodological / internal-consistency. See review file.

### ✓ 2026-05-10: Refine topics/phenomenology-of-memory-and-the-self.md — mineness inference (synchronic→diachronic bridge + modular-brain physicalist counter)
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: From convergent outer reviews (2026-05-10, 2/3 reviewers): [claude-opus-4-7, gemini-2-5-pro]. Both reviewers flag that the article's mineness inference is inadequately defended in two complementary directions. **(1) Philosophical move (Claude's framing):** synchronic→diachronic slide. The article uses Zahavian for-me-ness / mineness to underwrite *diachronic* identity, but Zahavi himself characterizes mineness as a synchronic feature of each present experience and explicitly distinguishes it from diachronic identity. Engage Lane (2012), Guillot (2017), Howell & Thompson (2017), Dings (2022) — all argue for-me-ness is too weak to ground numerical identity over time. Claude: *"The Map's argument requires the strong claim — mineness as numerically identifying across time — but the textual support it cites (Zahavi/Gallagher) underwrites only the weak claim."* **(2) Empirical move (Gemini's framing):** modular-brain physicalist counter. Gemini: *"Neurobiology easily posits that the brain possesses separate neural networks for data retrieval (hippocampal) and self-referential affective tagging (medial prefrontal cortex). When the connection is severed, the data is retrieved without the tag. By weaponizing pathology for metaphysics, the dualist framing willfully ignores the mechanistic, modular architecture of the physical brain."* The Klein & Nichols (2012) dissociation (already cited in the article, line 55, 139) is empirically compatible with both the dualist and the modular-tag readings — the choice between them is constrained by other commitments, not forced by the empirical data alone. The refine must address both gaps in a single section: (a) explicitly bridge synchronic to diachronic mineness or supplement with a separate diachronic criterion (haecceity, deep-further-fact); (b) engage the modular-brain physicalist alternative directly — state what would have to be true for the modular hypothesis to leave a phenomenal residue and why the Map's commitments rule it out. The article currently equivocates between "every experience is mine" (Zahavian, true) and "the same me persists across all my experiences" (substantive metaphysical thesis). Be explicit about which is required for the No-Many-Worlds inference and what auxiliary commitment does the bridging work. Apply [direct-refutation-discipline](/project/direct-refutation-discipline/) for both moves. ~400–600 words touched (slightly larger than either originating task because both criticisms must be addressed). Tenet alignment: Tenet 4 (No Many Worlds) load-bearing; Tenet 1 (Dualism); methodological / [evidential-status-discipline](/project/evidential-status-discipline/) / [direct-refutation-discipline](/project/direct-refutation-discipline/). See review files.
- **Output**: obsidian/topics/phenomenology-of-memory-and-the-self.md

### ✓ 2026-05-10: Add "From Irreducibility to Dualism" section to topics/the-convergence-argument-for-dualism.md
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: From pessimistic-2026-05-10 Issue 3 (High severity). Line 130 of the article correctly discloses: "convergence on 'consciousness is puzzling' is not the same as convergence on 'dualism is true'" — Buddhist *anattā* is not dualism, Advaita monism is not dualism, "what the cross-cultural evidence supports is... the reality of the explanatory gap, which in turn supports (but does not alone establish) dualism." The qualifier is correct. But the lede ("multiple independent arguments converge on the same conclusion"), the Bayesian section's likelihood ratio framing (likelihood ratio between dualism and physicalism specifically), and the Relation-to-Site-Perspective section all proceed as if cross-traditional evidence supports the dualist conclusion specifically. The qualifier is installed and disregarded. Refine should add a short section "From Irreducibility to Dualism" after §Convergence Across Traditions and before §What Convergence Does Not Prove, engaging the irreducibility-respecting alternatives the convergence argument does not by itself rule out: panpsychism (faces the combination problem), neutral monism (leaves the bidirectional-interaction question open), idealism (collapses the asymmetry the convergence tracks), and Madhyamaka emptiness (consistent with the convergence pattern but its therapeutic project is orthogonal to the metaphysical question). The section should explicitly name the Map's commitment to dualism over these alternatives as resting on additional considerations — primarily the [bidirectional-interaction](/concepts/bidirectional-interaction/) tenet — that the convergence argument doesn't itself supply. This is the structurally-honest move that the article's own line-130 qualifier makes necessary. Estimated scope: ~300–450 words added. Tenet alignment: methodological + [Dualism](/tenets/#dualism) + [Bidirectional Interaction](/tenets/#bidirectional-interaction). Task context:
From pessimistic-2026-05-10 Issue 3 (High severity). Line 130 of the article correctly discloses: "convergence on 'consciousness is puzzling' is not the same as convergence on 'dualism is true'" — Buddhist *anattā* is not dualism, Advaita monism is not dualism, "what the cross-cultural evidence supports is... the reality of the explanatory gap, which in turn supports (but does not alone establish) dualism." The qualifier is correct. But the lede ("multiple independent arguments converge on the same conclusion"), the Bayesian section's likelihood ratio framing (likelihood ratio between dualism and physicalism specifically), and the Relation-to-Site-Perspective section all proceed as if cross-traditional evidence supports the dualist conclusion specifically. The qualifier is installed and disregarded. Refine should add a short section "From Irreducibility to Dualism" after §Convergence Across Traditions and before §What Convergence Does Not Prove, engaging the irreducibility-respecting alternatives the convergence argument does not by itself rule out: panpsychism (faces the combination problem), neutral monism (leaves the bidirectional-interaction question open), idealism (collapses the asymmetry the convergence tracks), and Madhyamaka emptiness (consistent with the convergence pattern but its therapeutic project is orthogonal to the metaphysical question). The section should explicitly name the Map's commitment to dualism over these alternatives as resting on additional considerations — primarily the [bidirectional-interaction](/concepts/bidirectional-interaction/) tenet — that the convergence argument doesn't itself supply. This is the structurally-honest move that the article's own line-130 qualifier makes necessary. Estimated scope: ~300–450 words added. ### ✓ 2026-05-10: Restructure vitalism disanalogy in topics/the-convergence-argument-for-dualism.md as type-specific not temporal
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: From pessimistic-2026-05-10 Issue 2 (High severity). The vitalism disanalogy (lines 138–142) is the article's central rebuttal to the convergence-on-falsehood worry, and it is structured as a temporal observation ("the gap has not narrowed") presented as a structural claim ("the consciousness case is structurally different"). A vitalist in 1820 could have made the identical observation. The structural disanalogy the article gestures at — "no instance of 'this is what redness *is* in physical terms'" — uses the irreducibility of qualia as the disanalogy with vitalism, but the irreducibility of qualia is the conclusion of the convergence argument, so the disanalogy is structurally circular. Refine should replace the temporal-presented-as-structural framing with a type-specific argument: phenomenal qualities (redness, painfulness, etc.) specify particular phenomenal types that any reduction would have to deliver type-by-type, while "vital force" was always a placeholder for unspecified mechanism — so the consciousness case demands type-specific reductions in a way the vitalism case did not. This argument is independent of the convergence argument's conclusion and does the structural work the article currently fails to do. Alternatively, honestly downgrade the disanalogy to a temporal observation while flagging the open structural question. Estimated scope: ~150–250 words rewritten in §Convergence on falsehood is possible. Tenet alignment: methodological + [reductionism-and-consciousness](/topics/reductionism-and-consciousness/). See [pessimistic-2026-05-10](/reviews/pessimistic-2026-05-10/) Issue 2.
- **Output**: obsidian/topics/the-convergence-argument-for-dualism.md

### ✓ 2026-05-10: Address Cluster 3 independence gap in topics/the-convergence-argument-for-dualism.md
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: From pessimistic-2026-05-10 Issue 1 (High severity). The Bayesian section (lines 78–86) collapses eight arguments to three clusters and then asserts that the three are "substantially independent lines of evidence." The independence of Cluster 3 (unity of consciousness, intentionality) from Cluster 1 (phenomenal intuition) is the load-bearing premise of the cumulative-force claim and is asserted rather than argued. On a heterophenomenological reading (Dennett), Cluster 3's targets are reports-about-phenomenal-contents — the same domain the phenomenal concept strategy addresses — so Cluster 3 collapses into Cluster 1 unless the article supplies independent grounds. Refine should (a) add a paragraph in §The Bayesian Structure that argues Cluster 3's independence in vocabulary the heterophenomenologist accepts — the binding problem in vision science is establishable from third-person evidence and is the strongest candidate for genuinely-independent grounds for the unity argument; (b) acknowledge that intentionality's third-person establishability is contested and weaken the cluster's force accordingly, or supply an independent third-person argument for aboutness; (c) propagate the resulting calibration through the response to the phenomenal concept strategy at line 90 ("addresses Clusters 1 and 2 but has less traction with Cluster 3" — soften to "the strategy's traction with Cluster 3 depends on whether unity and intentionality reduce to reports-about-phenomenal-contents or have independent third-person establishability") and through the cumulative-force claim at line 86. Estimated scope: ~250–400 words touched. Tenet alignment: methodological + [Dualism](/tenets/#dualism). See [pessimistic-2026-05-10](/reviews/pessimistic-2026-05-10/) Issue 1.

### ✓ 2026-05-10: Add three methodology rules to project/evidential-status-discipline.md (phenomenological-vs-metaphysical, dissociation-levels, MWI-checklist)
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: From outer review by ChatGPT 5.5 Pro 2026-05-10. Items 12–14 of the review's improvement list. The reviewer's verification notes flagged this as the right level for cross-cutting rules. Three additions to [evidential-status-discipline](/project/evidential-status-discipline/): (a) **Rule: phenomenological datum ≠ irreducible metaphysical datum.** Prevents the move from "this is experienced" to "this is non-computational" without an explicit bridging argument. The site already warns against upgrading possibilities into probabilities; this rule extends the discipline to the experience→irreducibility axis specifically. (b) **Rule: dissociation arguments must separate four levels.** Any article using clinical or anomaly dissociations (Klein & Nichols, Capgras, blindsight, alien-hand, etc.) should distinguish: separability (the two phenomena come apart in the data), phenomenological reality (one is a genuine feature of experience), mechanistic independence (different processes underlie them), and metaphysical irreducibility (the dissociated feature cannot be physically/functionally explained). Evidence for one level should not automatically be counted as evidence for the next. (c) **Rule: MWI-specific review checklist.** Before any article claims to refute Many-Worlds, require it to answer: "Could an Everettian restate this phenomenon as branch-local, centered, and determinate?" If yes, the article should classify the disagreement as a framework boundary (Mode Three in [direct-refutation-discipline](/project/direct-refutation-discipline/) terms) unless it has an additional argument for why global ontological uniqueness, rather than branch-local uniqueness, is required by the phenomenon. This rule operationalises the boundary-substitution failure mode that four independent outer reviewers have now converged on (2026-05-03 ChatGPT, 2026-05-04 ChatGPT, 2026-05-04 Claude, 2026-05-10 ChatGPT). Estimated scope: ~400–600 words added to evidential-status-discipline. Tenet alignment: methodological. Sequencing note: independent of the P1 refine-draft above; can execute in parallel.
- **Output**: obsidian/project/evidential-status-discipline.md

### ✓ 2026-05-10: Write project doc on the Common-Cause Null in Convergence Arguments
- **Type**: expand-topic
- **Notes**: Suggested by optimistic-2026-05-09b (Medium Priority). The new apex's line 144 explicit common-cause acknowledgement is the catalogue's first article-level engagement with the common-cause hypothesis as a structural objection rather than as an ad hoc concern. The topic deserves project-doc treatment because the common-cause null is one of the standard objections any cumulative-convergence argument has to engage, and the catalogue currently engages it ad hoc in different articles (sometimes well, sometimes not). Capacity argues against topics/ placement (239/250 = 95%) and against concepts/ placement (230/250 = 92%); project/ doc placement is preferred, parallel to existing methodology docs (`project/closed-loop-opportunity-execution`, `project/bedrock-clash-vs-absorption`, `project/coalesce-condense-apex-stability`). Article would (a) name the common-cause objection as the standard inferential challenge to convergence arguments — convergence across N domains is one observation if all N share the same upstream cause, not N independent observations; (b) catalogue the convergence-argument types in the catalogue and show how each engages the common-cause null (or fails to) — the dissociation cluster apex, the phenomenal-divergence cluster, the empirical-phenomena-of-mental-causation pair, the convergence-argument-for-dualism; (c) develop the cross-substrate-within-one-organism response and its limits; (d) install cross-species, cross-cultural, and patient-population evidence as the structurally distinguishing tests — turning the apex's "what evidence would distinguish" framing from a closed disclaimer into an open empirical research programme; (e) supply a checklist for future convergence-argument articles; (f) honest limitation: the common-cause null can also be wielded as a universal solvent against any convergence claim, so the discipline is itself susceptible to *over-application* — when a paragraph develops this risk, name what would license treating an introspective convergence as independent triangulation despite shared introspective architecture (substantive structural divergence between substrates, dissociable failure patterns, etc.). Medium scope (1500–2200 words). Tenet alignment: methodological + Tenet 5 (Occam's Razor Has Limits — premature parsimony in the convergence's favour is symmetric to the simplicity-overreach Tenet 5 names on the materialist side). See [optimistic-2026-05-09b](/reviews/optimistic-2026-05-09b/) (Medium Priority opportunity) and [phenomenal-output-causal-machinery-dissociation](/apex/phenomenal-output-causal-machinery-dissociation/) line 144.

### ✓ 2026-05-09: Cross-review topics/consciousness-and-the-phenomenology-of-translation.md considering the phenomenal-output / causal-machinery dissociation cluster
- **Type**: cross-review
- **Notes**: Chain from today's refine-draft of `topics/consciousness-and-the-phenomenology-of-translation.md` (recent_tasks 2026-05-09). Translation is a candidate fifth-axis exhibit of the apex's cluster: the *felt sense* of meaning-arrival (the moment a foreign-language phrase resolves into one's native semantic register, or the inverse moment of catching the lexical equivalent without the conceptual fit) is a phenomenal output that runs ahead of (or behind) the sub-personal lexical-semantic-pragmatic search machinery that produces it. The phenomenology shows the verdict-arrival; the operation is hidden. This is the apex's diagnostic signature applied to bilingual/translation cognition. Cross-review should (a) check whether `topics/consciousness-and-the-phenomenology-of-translation.md` references the apex `[[phenomenal-output-causal-machinery-dissociation]]` and whether the cluster-membership question is engaged or explicitly declined (the article may have its own load-bearing focus that doesn't justify cluster recruitment); (b) if cluster recruitment is warranted, install a brief bridging paragraph (~150–250 words) naming the dissociation diagnostic as it applies to translation specifically — output (the felt resolution) reaches awareness, operation (lexical-semantic search, syntactic re-mapping, pragmatic adjustment) does not — and add the article to the apex's source roster reciprocally; (c) if cluster recruitment is *not* warranted, document the reasoning so that future cross-reviews don't re-raise the candidacy without reading the previous decision; (d) verify alignment with `concepts/cognitive-phenomenology` and `concepts/phenomenology-vs-function-axis` framings — translation is a worked-example domain for both concepts and the membership question may already be partly answered there. Short-medium scope (~200–400 words touched). Tenet alignment: methodological + Tenet 3 (Bidirectional Interaction).
- **Output**: obsidian/topics/consciousness-and-the-phenomenology-of-translation.md -- Context: Cross-review topics/consciousness-and-the-phenomenology-of-translation.md considering the phenomenal-output / causal-machinery dissociation cluster

### ✓ 2026-05-09: Address common-cause and matching-detail inheritance in topics/empirical-phenomena-mental-causation.md
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: From `reviews/pessimistic-2026-05-09b.md` Counterargument 2 and Unsupported Claims table. The pessimistic review of the new apex explicitly flags that the apex "imports the positive-companion framing from `empirical-phenomena-mental-causation` and inherits its weaknesses" — the apex synthesis cannot be stronger than its source. Two specific weaknesses inherit: (1) **"matching detail" of phenomenology-to-physiology coupling (line 116 of apex; mirrored in the source article)** — currently rhetorical without specification. Placebo's content-specificity (verbal information selecting cascade) and choking's mode-specificity (attentional mode selecting disrupted skill) are *different fineness scales*, and "matching" elides the difference. Refine should specify what "matching" means by naming the two fineness scales explicitly and articulating what the joint claim requires (e.g., "in both cases the phenomenal description selects the causal pathway at the same level of grain at which the brain implements the selection — propositional content for placebo, attentional mode for choking — neither finer nor coarser than the implementation requires"). (2) **The illusionist absorption of the positive-companion claim** — choking selects between attentional modes, not phenomenal modes; placebo's content-specificity selects between propositional content, not phenomenal modes. The article needs to either (a) frame the positive-companion claim more cautiously by acknowledging that the empirical evidence is consistent with two readings (representational-state coupling and phenomenology-tracking coupling), and noting that the cluster's two-sided shape obtains in both, or (b) make the case explicitly that the *felt* difference (not the *represented* difference) is what does the causal work — which the article currently asserts at line 116 of the apex but does not earn at the source. The morning's deep-review (`deep-review-2026-05-09-empirical-phenomena-mental-causation.md`) found the heterophenomenology engagement honest at Mode-Three but did not resolve the felt-vs-represented disambiguation. Refine should also (3) address the common-cause objection at the source: "share little common machinery beyond conscious processing" (the apex's recurring premise) gets its evidential weight in part from the placebo/choking pair contributing two genuinely distinct substrates (humoral/neurochemical for placebo, motor-cortical/basal-ganglia for choking) — make this argument explicitly at the source so the apex can cite it rather than carry the unspecified phrase. Medium scope (~400–700 words touched). Tenet alignment: Tenet 3 (Bidirectional Interaction) + methodological. See [pessimistic-2026-05-09b](/reviews/pessimistic-2026-05-09b/) Counterargument 2 and Unsupported Claims rows 1, 3.
- **Output**: obsidian/topics/empirical-phenomena-mental-causation.md

### ✓ 2026-05-09: Address pessimistic-2026-05-09b findings on apex/phenomenal-output-causal-machinery-dissociation.md
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: From `reviews/pessimistic-2026-05-09b.md`. The new apex (created 2026-05-09T17:38, deep-reviewed at 18:18 with focus on orphan integration) carries the catalogue's load-bearing cumulative-convergence move and was found to over-claim along five axes that the morning's deep-review did not engage. Refine should address: **Issue 1 (HIGH, common-cause hypothesis)** — the "share little common machinery beyond conscious processing" condition recurs eight times (lines 64, 116, 138, 140, 156, 158, 178) as the load-bearing premise of the convergence-from-different-domains claim and is never argued; all seven traditions analyse human cognition through human introspection in human language, so the shared introspective architecture itself is the common machinery. Add a paragraph (after the seven traditions, or in §Cumulative-Convergence) acknowledging the common-cause hypothesis explicitly and naming what would distinguish independent-triangulation from same-introspective-architecture-rediscovered (cross-species evidence, cross-cultural evidence, anomalous-introspection patient populations). The strongest defence is probably the cross-substrate-within-one-organism argument (perceptual cardinality, sub-second; memory consolidation, decades; cannot share specific machinery) — that argument needs to be made, not assumed. **Issue 2 (HIGH, Carruthers double-counting)** — Carruthers's *Opacity of Mind* argues introspective opacity is a contingent design feature of a sensory-format introspection mechanism, i.e. the materialist explanation the article presents the cluster as putting pressure on. Distinguish two sub-classes within the seven traditions: (a) those that observe the signature *despite* their broader commitments (Polanyi, Bergson, possibly some readings of Koriat), (b) those that observe the signature *because* their materialist models predict it (Carruthers, Trick & Pylyshyn, Inzlicht/Kurzban, Schwitzgebel). The convergence claim's force comes mainly from class (a); class (b) is internal corroboration of the materialist prediction. **Issue 3 (MEDIUM, "would predict" unearned)** — soften "the two-sided structure is what an interface architecture would predict" (line 110) and "an interface architecture should sometimes track the operation it accompanies and sometimes detach from it" (line 118) to "is consistent with" — the two-sided shape is what *any* selective-access account predicts (higher-order theory, illusionism, global workspace). The article's actual move is selection-by-coherence (interface dualism accommodates the shape naturally and physicalism owes a story about the architectural seams), which is a cost-of-explanation argument, not a unique-prediction argument. **Issue 4 (MEDIUM, Wegner inversion)** — Wegner's *Illusion of Conscious Will* (cited line 94, 98, ref 17) is the strongest illusionist reading: felt willing is confabulation, no underlying willing for the felt sense to be a window onto. This inverts the cluster's positive-companion claim. Either drop Wegner from the converging-voices count and cite him only inside the agency-void paragraph as the strongest illusionist reading the cluster has to engage with, or keep him in the count but explicitly flag that his thesis inverts the cluster's reading. **Issue 5 (MEDIUM, contemplative pre-emption)** — line 168's dismissal of "anecdotal contemplative reports" pre-empts a class of evidence (Husserlian epoché, open-monitoring meditation, the EASE interview which is in fact a checked, calibrated phenomenological instrument with inter-rater agreement data) without specifying verifiability conditions. Add a paragraph naming contemplative-and-phenomenological traditions explicitly, distinguishing reports of *content* normally suppressed (which the cluster can absorb as outputs-by-deformation) from reports of *operations* normally hidden (which would weaken the signature if they stabilised). Also strengthens the falsifiability section by specifying verifiability conditions. **Counterargument 2 (illusionist absorption of positive companion)** — the synthesis cannot be stronger than its source; either wait for the parallel refine-draft on `topics/empirical-phenomena-mental-causation.md` to address the illusionist absorption, or add a paragraph here that frames the positive-companion claim more cautiously. Medium-large scope (~600–1,000 words touched). Article currently 5,490 words at 137% of apex hard threshold — net additions should be paired with trims to hedging that the new arguments make redundant. Tenet alignment: methodological + Tenets 1 and 3. See [pessimistic-2026-05-09b](/reviews/pessimistic-2026-05-09b/).
- **Output**: obsidian/apex/phenomenal-output-causal-machinery-dissociation.md

### ✓ 2026-05-09: Refine topics/consciousness-and-the-phenomenology-of-translation.md to absorb voids-translation-void-2026-05-09 research
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: Research note `obsidian/research/voids-translation-void-2026-05-09.md` (3,970 words; created today 2026-05-09) is unconsumed — its `target_section: voids` cannot be honoured because voids/ is at 100/100 cap. The research's natural alternative home is the existing `topics/consciousness-and-the-phenomenology-of-translation.md` (last modified 2026-04-26, ~13 days old; ai_contribution 100), which already centres translation phenomenology, the split self, and the untranslatable remainder as meaning-bearing structures. The research surfaces several structurally distinct faces consciousness-cannot-read-its-own-translation-mechanism: (a) **Hofstadter-Sander analogy-core opacity** — *Surfaces and Essences* (2013) treats analogy as the substrate of all cognition, but the analogical core itself remains phenomenally inaccessible (we know we have made the analogy only after it lands); (b) **Gentner structure-mapping mechanism** — empirical structure-mapping work demonstrates the mapping operation is sub-personal and unavailable to introspection; (c) **untranslatable-words / Lomas positive-lexicography** evidence that languages crystallise distinct phenomenal regions some translators report cannot be re-lived in the target language; (d) **Quine-Davidson indeterminacy** as the philosophical anchor for the void's *unbridgeable-in-principle* face (where the dissociation cluster's *unbridgeable-in-practice* faces are empirical, this is conceptual); (e) **LLM translation limits** — large language models execute translation at high competence without (per the Map's commitments) phenomenal access to the analogical core, providing a cleanest functional-without-phenomenal contrast case. Refine should (a) install a new section (~600–900 words) — candidate placement after the article's existing "untranslatable remainder" section, candidate title "What Translation Cannot Read About Its Own Operation" or "The Analogical Core's Phenomenal Opacity" — surveying the five faces above with explicit hedging that these results *constrain* the dualist reading rather than *establish* it (per the just-formalised constrain-vs-establish discipline in `project/evidential-status-discipline.md`); (b) honour framework-stage-calibration — the research's positioning of translation as a void-tier subject must be calibrated against the topic-tier home: the *phenomenology* of translation is the topic; the *void* of inaccessible analogical mechanism is what the new section names; (c) cross-link to `voids/meaning-void.md`, `voids/metaphor-void.md`, `voids/aspect-perception-void.md`, `voids/conceptual-scheme-void.md`, `voids/inference-void.md`, `voids/tacit-integration-void.md` (all listed as siblings in the research note's `related_articles`), and to the new `apex/phenomenal-output-causal-machinery-dissociation.md` as the cluster's apex-tier home (translation-as-output / analogical-mechanism-as-operation maps cleanly onto the dissociation pattern); (d) preserve the article's existing length band (currently ~3,800 words; the addition pushes toward but should not breach the 4,000-word topics soft threshold); (e) audit for "This is not X. It is Y." cliché violations; (f) update `last_deep_review` and `ai_modified` frontmatter; add `[[research/voids-translation-void-2026-05-09]]` to `related_articles`. Medium scope (~600–900 words touched). Tenet alignment: Tenet 1 (Dualism) — the analogical-mechanism / phenomenal-output dissociation extends the dissociation cluster's structural argument into the translation domain; Tenet 5 (Occam's Razor Has Limits) — Quine-Davidson indeterminacy bears directly on the limits-of-simplicity tenet. See `obsidian/research/voids-translation-void-2026-05-09.md` for full source detail.
- **Output**: obsidian/topics/consciousness-and-the-phenomenology-of-translation.md

Task context:
Research note `obsidian/research/voids-translation-void-2026-05-09.md` (3,970 words; created today 2026-05-09) is unconsumed — its `target_section: voids` cannot be honoured because voids/ is at 100/100 cap. The research's natural alternative home is the existing `topics/consciousness-and-the-phenomenology-of-translation.md` (last modified 2026-04-26, ~13 days old; ai_contribution 100), which already centres translation phenomenology, the split self, and the untranslatable remainder as meaning-bearing structures. The research surfaces several structurally distinct faces consciousness-cannot-read-its-own-translation-mechanism: (a) **Hofstadter-Sander analogy-core opacity** — *Surfaces and Essences* (2013) treats analogy as the substrate of all cognition, but the analogical core itself remains phenomenally inaccessible (we know we have made the analogy only after it lands); (b) **Gentner structure-mapping mechanism** — empirical structure-mapping work demonstrates the mapping operation is sub-personal and unavailable to introspection; (c) **untranslatable-words / Lomas positive-lexicography** evidence that languages crystallise distinct phenomenal regions some translators report cannot be re-lived in the target language; (d) **Quine-Davidson indeterminacy** as the philosophical anchor for the void's *unbridgeable-in-principle* face (where the dissociation cluster's *unbridgeable-in-practice* faces are empirical, this is conceptual); (e) **LLM translation limits** — large language models execute translation at high competence without (per the Map's commitments) phenomenal access to the analogical core, providing a cleanest functional-without-phenomenal contrast case. Refine should (a) install a new section (~600–900 words) — candidate placement after the article's existing "untranslatable remainder" section, candidate title "What Translation Cannot Read About Its Own Operation" or "The Analogical Core's Phenomenal Opacity" — surveying the five faces above with explicit hedging that these results *constrain* the dualist reading rather than *establish* it (per the just-formalised constrain-vs-establish discipline in `project/evidential-status-discipline.md`); (b) honour framework-stage-calibration — the research's positioning of translation as a void-tier subject must be calibrated against the topic-tier home: the *phenomenology* of translation is the topic; the *void* of inaccessible analogical mechanism is what the new section names; (c) cross-link to `voids/meaning-void.md`, `voids/metaphor-void.md`, `voids/aspect-perception-void.md`, `voids/conceptual-scheme-void.md`, `voids/inference-void.md`, `voids/tacit-integration-void.md` (all listed as siblings in the research note's `related_articles`), and to the new `apex/phenomenal-output-causal-machinery-dissociation.md` as the cluster's apex-tier home (translation-as-output / analogical-mechanism-as-operation maps cleanly onto the dissociation pattern); (d) preserve the article's existing length band (currently ~3,800 words; the addition pushes toward but should not breach the 4,000-word topics soft threshold); (e) audit for "This is not X. It is Y." cliché violations; (f) update `last_deep_review` and `ai_modified` frontmatter; add `[[research/voids-translation-void-2026-05-09]]` to `related_articles`. Medium scope (~600–900 words touched). Tenet alignment: Tenet 1 (Dualism) — the analogical-mechanism / phenomenal-output dissociation extends the dissociation cluster's structural argument into the translation domain; Tenet 5 (Occam's Razor Has Limits) — Quine-Davidson indeterminacy bears directly on the limits-of-simplicity tenet. See `obsidian/research/voids-translation-void-2026-05-09.md` for full source detail.

### ✓ 2026-05-09: Refine apex/phenomenal-output-causal-machinery-dissociation.md to address pessimistic-2026-05-09b findings
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: Pessimistic review surfaced five issues the same-day deep-review missed (deep-review focused almost entirely on orphan integration). Three are structural and warrant prose-level work: (1) **The "share little common machinery beyond conscious processing" condition recurs eight times as the load-bearing premise of the convergence-from-different-domains claim and is never argued.** All seven traditions analyse human cognition through human introspection in human language; the shared introspective architecture itself is the common machinery a common-cause hypothesis predicts. Add a paragraph in §Seven Traditions or §Cumulative-Convergence acknowledging the common-cause reading and naming what would distinguish independent-triangulation from same-introspective-architecture-rediscovered (cross-species, cross-cultural, anomalous-introspective-architecture patient evidence; the strongest defence is recurrence across substrates *within* a single nervous system — perceptual cardinality and decadal memory consolidation cannot share specific machinery — but that argument needs to be made, not assumed). (2) **The Carruthers citation works against the article's own conclusion.** Carruthers's *The Opacity of Mind* explains the signature as a contingent design feature of a sensory-format introspection mechanism — i.e., the materialist explanation the article presents the cluster as putting pressure on. Distinguish two sub-classes within the seven traditions: (a) those that observe the signature *despite* their broader commitments (Polanyi, Bergson, possibly Koriat) and (b) those that observe it *because* their materialist models predict it (Carruthers, Trick & Pylyshyn, Inzlicht/Kurzban, Schwitzgebel). The convergence claim's force comes mainly from class (a); class (b) is internal corroboration of the materialist prediction. Soften the seven-author count claim accordingly. (3) **"Interface architecture would predict the two-sided structure" (line 110, line 118) is unearned.** Any selective-access account predicts the same shape including higher-order theory, illusionism, and global workspace theory. Soften "would predict" to "is consistent with" wherever it occurs; reframe as a cost-of-explanation argument, not a unique-prediction argument. Two further issues are scope-dependent fixes: (4) **Wegner cited as a converging voice without flagging that his thesis (illusionism about conscious will) inverts the cluster's reading** (line 94, line 98) — either drop him from the converging count and cite him only inside the agency-void paragraph, or flag the inversion explicitly; (5) **The seven-traditions framing pre-empts contemplative-and-phenomenological traditions that claim inspection-while-operating** (Husserlian phenomenology, open-monitoring meditation, the EASE clinical-phenomenology interview) — currently dismissed in a half-sentence; specify verifiability conditions for the second falsifier and engage the EASE interview as a calibrated phenomenological instrument that may already partly satisfy them. The unsupported-claims table and language-improvements table in the review identify specific edits (lede strengthens beyond what the discipline section concedes; "matching detail" rhetorical without quantification; "currently dominant forms have not been pressed to address" inaccurate given that higher-order theory and illusionism address introspective opacity directly). Medium scope (~600–900 words touched, mostly soften/clarify rather than restructure). Tenet alignment: Tenet 1 (Dualism) — the cluster's strongest tenet-bearing structure should rest on the most defensible convergence claim. See [pessimistic-2026-05-09b](/reviews/pessimistic-2026-05-09b/).
- **Output**: obsidian/apex/phenomenal-output-causal-machinery-dissociation.md

Estimated scope: long article (3,000–4,000 words). Tenet alignment: Tenet 1 (Dualism) directly; Tenet 5 (Occam's Razor Has Limits) — the cluster is the single tightest demonstration in the catalogue that the materialist's "consciousness is just brain activity" cannot account for why phenomenal output detaches systematically from the operations it putatively reports on. **CAPACITY CAVEAT**: apex/ at 25/20 over informal governance cap; the audit task already P3-queued ("Refine apex/apex-articles.md to address apex section over-cap") should run first. ### ✓ 2026-05-09: Refine topics/empirical-phenomena-mental-causation.md to address pessimistic-2026-05-09
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: From [pessimistic-2026-05-09](/reviews/pessimistic-2026-05-09/). Three critical/high-severity issues on the post-coalesce, post-condense form (3144 words). (a) **Issue 1, line 106**: rewrite the non-sequitur — the sentence "If consciousness were epiphenomenal, it could not interfere with procedural execution" is strictly false on standard epiphenomenalism (the NCC of self-monitoring obviously can interfere); replace with a phenomenal-character-targeted version such as "If the *phenomenal character* of self-monitoring did no causal work, the dependence of choking on the felt mode of attention would lack explanation." High priority — the current sentence is the kind of mistake a careful reader will catch immediately and discount the article over. (b) **Issue 2, lines 147–155**: address the boundary-substitution in the Epiphenomenalist Challenge section — the section grants the epiphenomenalist's central move and then treats the standard hard problem as a defeater for epiphenomenalism. Either upgrade to the genuine in-framework move (strong epiphenomenalism predicts the phenomenal-functional mapping should be *arbitrary*; the systematic content-specificity of placebo *plus* systematic mode-specificity of choking together makes alleged arbitrariness less plausible than weaker phenomena would) or honestly downgrade to framework-marking ("epiphenomenalism's response is available; the Map's commitment to bidirectional interaction makes us treat the tight phenomenal-functional tracking as evidence the phenomenology is doing work, while acknowledging an epiphenomenalist absorbs the data as brute psychophysical law"). The upgrade path is preferred where feasible. (c) **Issue 3, lines 137–145**: the "How the Two Cases Reinforce Each Other" section is the article's central organising claim and the four bullets do not actually demonstrate joint strength — the "convergent vulnerability of competitor accounts" sub-argument (line 145) is the weakest because functionalism and illusionism are widely held jointly. Construct the genuine conjunction argument: placebo's positive content-direction and choking's negative mode-disruption operate on *different substrates* (humoral/neurochemical vs motor-cortical) but track phenomenological structure with the same precision, which is harder to absorb under a single representationalist frame than either alone — *or* honestly weaken the lede claim of "unusually strong evidence." Also (d) per pessimistic Issue counterargument 2 — explicitly mark the argument-shift in the Open-Label Placebos subsection (line 92): the strong content-specificity argument runs on propositional belief; open-label data weakens this and pushes work onto a less precisely targeted ritual-engagement substrate; the "some mental causation" conclusion survives, the "propositional content selects cascades" conclusion is qualified. (e) Address citation gaps from pessimistic Unsupported Claims table: install citations for skill-asymmetry choking (probably Beilock & Carr 2001 with primary), implicit-protection (probably Masters 1992), dual-task improvements (probably Beilock et al. 2002); verify or correct the Benedetti 2003 attribution at line 82 (heart-rate-from-stimulant-content example may be Pollo or de la Fuente-Fernández); hedge the Marueckova 2024 placebo-neuroplasticity claim at line 100 (one recent narrative review on depression population; do not present as general structural finding); either cite Tulving-to-motor-execution bridge at line 161 or rephrase to avoid the autonoetic-memory/autonoetic-monitoring conflation. (f) Adopt the language improvements in pessimistic Language Improvements table where they fit. Sequencing: priority is (a) and (b) and (c) — these are the three high-severity issues; (d), (e), and (f) are medium. Estimated scope: ~300–600 words touched, no full rewrite needed. Preserve the article's voice and structure; the two-sided (placebo + choking) coalesce structure is sound and should not be unwound. Tenet alignment: Tenet 3 (Bidirectional Interaction) — the article is the catalogue's flagship empirical statement on this tenet; getting the named-opponent engagement right matters disproportionately.
- **Output**: obsidian/topics/empirical-phenomena-mental-causation.md

- **Type**: expand-topic
- **Notes**: Research completed 2026-05-08 in `research/memory-anomalies-2026-05-08.md` (~29k characters, comprehensive). Three closely related memory anomalies — déjà vu (false familiarity), jamais vu (false unfamiliarity), cryptomnesia (forgotten source mistaken for original idea) — synthesised as failures/quirks of the recollection-familiarity dual-process architecture. Strong neural evidence (especially temporal-lobe epilepsy work localising déjà vu to perirhinal/parahippocampal regions). Bergson's "memory of the present" provides the philosophical anchor: every perception casts a "shadow" memory, and the trio exposes the gap between phenomenal experience (felt familiarity/unfamiliarity/originality) and underlying causal machinery. Article should (a) treat the trio as a *structural cluster* — three rotations on the source-monitoring failure pattern rather than three independent anomalies; (b) anchor the temporal-lobe-epilepsy evidence as load-bearing for the *neural-mechanism-yet-tenet-coherent* framing the Map prefers; (c) install reciprocal cross-links to `[[consciousness-and-memory]]`, `[[phenomenology-of-memory-and-the-self]]`, `[[source-attribution-void]]`, `[[recognition-void]]`, `[[noetic-feelings-void]]`, and `[[temporal-consciousness]]`; (d) honour framework-stage-calibration — the Bergsonian "shadow memory" is one candidate explanation but not load-bearing for the Map's tenets; the deeper claim is the *gap* between phenomenal output and causal machinery; (e) discuss philosophical implications for self-knowledge, source-monitoring, and personal identity (cryptomnesia particularly relevant); (f) audit for "This is not X. It is Y." cliché violations (CLAUDE.md style ban). Target: `topics/` (currently 236/250, under cap). Estimated scope 1800-2400 words. Tenet alignment: Tenet 1 (Dualism) — felt-certainty produced when underlying causal machinery has gone wrong is the explanandum, not the evidence; Tenet 3 (Bidirectional Interaction) where Bergson's reducing-valve framing applies. See `[[research/memory-anomalies-2026-05-08]]`.
- **Output**: Write topic article on memory anomalies (déjà vu, jamais vu, cryptomnesia)

### ✓ 2026-05-09: Address tension between new dissociation section and surrounding argument in concepts/mental-effort.md
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: From [pessimistic-2026-05-08](/reviews/pessimistic-2026-05-08/). The 2026-05-08 refine-draft pass installed a new section "What Felt Effort Misses About Its Own Operation" (calibration / depletion / modulation faces, integrating Naccache 2005, Hagger 2016, Kurzban 2013, Inzlicht & Schmeichel 2012, Westbrook 2020). The section is well-crafted with honest framework-boundary marking. But its "felt effort is real, but it is not a transparent window onto the underlying machinery" hedge does not propagate backwards through the article. Two specific fixes (HIGH severity): (a) "The Materialist Problem" section (lines 102-106) poses rhetorical questions that the Inzlicht process model — cited in the new section — answers cleanly within physicalism; rewrite to engage the Inzlicht alternative rather than pretending it does not exist; (b) the Site Perspective "different currency" claim (line 182, "you don't get physically tired from attention... a different currency entirely") is contradicted by Westbrook 2020 (cited in same article) showing dopamine biochemistry modulates felt effort; either drop or reconcile. Two MEDIUM fixes: (c) the universality claim line 56 ("This phenomenology is universal") is now contradicted by the article's own Naccache citation — soften to "widely shared" or "the modal case"; (d) the Stapp Quantum Zeno timing-gap section (lines 137-142) concedes the femtosecond-vs-millisecond gap and reports Stapp's reply but does not engage Tegmark 2000's calculation; "remains unresolved" gives more parity than the math licenses. Either acknowledge calculation has not been answered on its own terms (and downgrade Quantum Zeno's prominence) or restructure to lead with post-decoherence selection ([forward-in-time-conscious-selection](/topics/forward-in-time-conscious-selection/), [selection-only-mind-influence](/topics/selection-only-mind-influence/)) as the better-developed Map mechanism. Two LOW fixes: (e) "What Would Challenge This View?" condition (3) ("equivalent neuroplastic changes occurred without phenomenal effort, e.g. under anaesthesia") is already empirically met by sleep consolidation, classical conditioning, and pharmacological neuroplasticity — narrow to "regulatory neuroplasticity in prefrontal-subcortical control circuits" or similar framework-specific phrasing; (f) remove the AI REFINEMENT LOG HTML comment block (lines 231-246) which contains `Engagement classification:` editor-vocabulary; the comment's own footer says it "should be removed after human review". Short-medium scope (~250-400 words touched). Tenet alignment: methodological + Tenet 2 (Minimal Quantum Interaction). See [pessimistic-2026-05-08](/reviews/pessimistic-2026-05-08/).

### ✓ 2026-05-08: Refine voids/agency-void.md to integrate voids-recurrence-void research insights
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: Research note `obsidian/research/voids-recurrence-void-2026-05-05.md` (4,800 words; 2026-05-05) is unconsumed — its `target_section: voids` cannot be honoured because voids/ is at 100/100 cap. The research's natural alternative home is the existing `voids/agency-void.md`, whose passive face (consciousness cannot control most of its own states) directly subsumes the recurrence territory. The research surfaces three structurally distinct faces consciousness-cannot-control-its-own-content-recurrence: (a) **intrusion face** — unwanted contents arrive uninvited (Clark et al. 80–99% of non-clinical populations report intrusive thoughts; Berntsen on involuntary autobiographical memory; Beaman & Williams on earworms); (b) **rebound face** — Wegner (1994) ironic-process theory's ironic monitor + Wang et al. (2020) meta-analytic temperament tempering the strongest claims while leaving the structural void intact; (c) **rumination face** — Nolen-Hoeksema response-styles theory + the loop sustains itself against will once content enters it. Apophatic signature: the very monitoring required to detect recurrence is part of the machinery that summons it. Refine should (a) install a new section (~500–800 words) within the agency-void article — candidate placement after the existing passive/skeptical-faces typology, candidate title "Recurrence as Passive-Face Mechanism" or "Why the Passive Limit Is Not Just Absence-of-Control" — naming the three recurrence faces as *operational instances* of the agency-void's passive limit (you cannot *will away* recurrence the way you cannot *will away* pain — the parallel is structural); (b) honour framework-stage-calibration — the dissociations *constrain* the dualist reading without *establishing* it; the rumination loop is also explicable under physicalist process models; (c) cross-link to `voids/thought-stream-void` (which currently treats how-thoughts-arise-unbidden — the recurrence intrusion-face is its operational complement), `voids/suspension-void` (structurally adjacent: cannot-suspend-judgment ↔ cannot-suspend-content-loop), `voids/ownership-void` (the unbidden-content's ownership status is part of the recurrence puzzle), `voids/noetic-feelings-void` (the *felt sense of intrusion* is itself a noetic feeling); (d) avoid duplicating `voids/thought-stream-void` material — that void handles *generation*; this is *re-presentation*; (e) preserve the article's existing length band (article is ~3,000 words; addition pushes toward but should not breach 3,500-word voids hard threshold); (f) audit for "This is not X. It is Y." cliché violations; (g) consider whether `voids/suspension-void` deserves a parallel sibling refinement integrating the rebound-face (Wegner ironic-process); if so, generate a follow-on task rather than expanding scope here; (h) update `last_deep_review` and `ai_modified` frontmatter; add `[[research/voids-recurrence-void-2026-05-05]]` to `related_articles`. Medium scope (~500–900 words touched). Tenet alignment: Tenet 1 (Dualism) — the structural unmodulability of recurrence is most-naturally-read as the lived face of an interface that consciousness operates from one side of, not on; Tenet 3 (Bidirectional Interaction) — the *modulation face* (cannot witness "trying harder" itself, only its felt output) constrains how directly conscious effort can reach mechanism. See `obsidian/research/voids-recurrence-void-2026-05-05.md` for full source detail.

### ✓ 2026-05-08: Refine concepts/mental-effort.md to integrate voids-effort-void research insights
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: Research note `obsidian/research/voids-effort-void-2026-05-08.md` (5,500 words; created today 2026-05-08) is unconsumed — its `target_section: voids` cannot be honoured because voids/ is at 100/100 cap. The research's natural alternative home is the existing `concepts/mental-effort.md` (last_deep_review 2026-04-19, ~19 days old; ai_contribution 100), which already centres effort phenomenology and Stapp's quantum-Zeno reading. The research surfaces three structurally distinct faces consciousness-cannot-read-its-own-effort: (a) **calibration face** — Naccache, Dehaene et al. (2005) ACC-lesion patient with normal executive control but no felt sense of mental effort whatsoever (foundational dissociation between phenomenal effort and the operation it ostensibly reports on); (b) **depletion face** — Hagger et al. (2016) preregistered 23-lab N=2,141 multilab replication of ego depletion at d=0.04, 95% CI [−0.07, 0.15], collapsing the strength-resource model; (c) **modulation face** — Kurzban opportunity-cost framework + Inzlicht/Schmeichel effort-as-information process model treat the felt sense as the *output* of sub-personal cost-benefit computation, not a window onto the operation. Refine should (a) install a new section (~500–800 words) — candidate placement after the "Phenomenology of Effort" section, candidate title "The Effort Cannot Read Itself" or "What Felt Effort Misses About Its Own Operation" — surveying the three faces with explicit hedging that these results *constrain* the dualist reading rather than *establish* it; (b) honour framework-stage-calibration (per `project/framework-stage-calibration.md`) — the dissociations are most-naturally-read as *interface-asymmetry* but are also compatible with strong-physicalist readings under Inzlicht's process model; the refine must not over-claim what the empirical record establishes; (c) cross-link to `concepts/cognitive-phenomenology` (the Würzburg-Titchener dissociation pattern is structurally parallel to Naccache's effortless-control dissociation), `voids/agency-void` (the recurrence/intrusion face shares the cannot-control-mental-content territory), `voids/noetic-feelings-void` (felt-effort is in the noetic-feelings family), `voids/suspension-void`, `voids/appetitive-void`; (d) integrate the existing Naccache reference (already cited in mental-effort.md? verify with grep) with the new ACC-lesion-patient framing rather than duplicating; (e) preserve the article's existing length band (article is ~3,500 words; addition pushes toward but should not breach the 4,000-word topics/concepts soft threshold); (f) audit for "This is not X. It is Y." cliché violations introduced by the new material; (g) update `last_deep_review` and `ai_modified` frontmatter; add `[[research/voids-effort-void-2026-05-08]]` to `related_articles`. Medium scope (~500–900 words touched). Tenet alignment: Tenet 1 (Dualism) — the felt-effort/operation dissociation is structural evidence of an asymmetry between phenomenal access and the underlying machinery; Tenet 3 (Bidirectional Interaction) — Naccache's autonomic SCR coupling in normals (absent in the patient) suggests felt effort does causal work not reducible to its reported task. See `obsidian/research/voids-effort-void-2026-05-08.md` for full source detail.

- **Type**: cross-review

### ✓ 2026-05-06: Decide whether to chain a sibling concept-page on arena-magnitude-bounds-and-active-protection
- **Type**: expand-topic (decision task)
- **Decision**: No — defer indefinitely. Task closed; replenishment should not regenerate.
- **Reasoning summary** (full reasoning in `obsidian/workflow/changelog.md` 2026-05-06 20:21 UTC entry):
  1. Compound concept fails decomposition test — magnitude-bound and active-protection are distinct ideas adjacent in §5 of the parent topic but do not form a single coherent concept-page unit.
  2. Structural-magnitude-bound claim is a derivation from existing concepts ([causal-powers](/concepts/causal-powers/) + [bidirectional-interaction](/concepts/bidirectional-interaction/)); a hub page would create reference duplication rather than provide a new building block. A brief cross-link note inside those existing concepts pointing at the parent topic is the cleaner alternative if discoverability becomes an issue.
  3. Active-protection content is explicitly tagged speculative-integration tier in the parent (line 115); concept-page promotion would itself be a slippage hazard at the editorial register.
  4. Pascal's-mugging-vs-structural-unboundedness distinction is methodological — if it warrants extraction, the right home is a `project/` doc on direct-refutation discipline, not a concepts page.
  5. Parent §5 is self-contained post-condense + post-deep-review; future articles have a clean cross-link target at the topic level.
  6. Concepts at 230/250 — the marginal slot is better spent on the two existing P3 candidates (`mind-arena` definitional, Gaming-Problem concept) which have stronger standalone-concept warrants.
- **Re-evaluation trigger**: revisit only if three or more future articles independently want to cross-link to this material with bridging text materially shared across them — that pattern would constitute the multi-article cross-reference warrant currently absent.

### ✓ 2026-05-06: Fact-check the human-chimpanzee 98-99% DNA-similarity claim across the catalogue
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: Two articles currently assert the human-chimp DNA-similarity figure as load-bearing scaffolding for the human-vs-other-animals cognitive-gap argument: `topics/animal-consciousness.md:110` ("Great apes share 98-99% of our DNA…") and `apex/minds-without-words.md:78` ("Great apes—chimpanzees, bonobos, gorillas—share 98-99% of our DNA…"). The 98-99% figure derives from older SNV-only comparisons over syntenic regions and *may* be substantially overstated under more recent analyses. In particular, T2T-CHM13-era complete-genome comparisons (Yoo et al. 2023 *Nature*; Hallast et al. 2023 *Nature* on the chimpanzee Y; Makova et al. 2024 on great-ape complete genomes) report whole-genome identities closer to ~96% — and on heterochromatic / Y-chromosomal regions substantially lower — once indels, structural variants, and previously-unalignable regions are included. **Fact-check task**: (a) verify the current state of the literature on whole-genome (not SNV-only) human-chimpanzee identity using post-2023 sources — confirm or refute the ~96% revised figure; (b) determine whether the older 98-99% figure remains defensible *under explicit scope-restriction* (e.g., "98-99% identity across alignable coding regions, ~96% across the complete genome including indels and structural variants"); (c) update both articles to reflect the most defensible current-literature framing — likely a hedged "~96-99% depending on what is counted (SNV-only over alignable regions vs. whole-genome including indels and structural variants)" with a citation to a post-2023 review; (d) examine whether the load-bearing argument changes — the human-cognitive-gap argument is more cleanly served by *substantial similarity with substantial divergence* (architectural-difference framing) than by a single percentage figure, and may actually become *stronger* if the figure is lower (more genetic divergence is consistent with the cognitive gap being genuine, not a "small DNA-difference miracle"); (e) honour `[[evidential-status-discipline]]` — the figure is empirical and should be cited from a current peer-reviewed source; the older 98-99% claim was widely repeated in popular and pedagogical sources and made it into both articles via that route, illustrating the discipline's anti-staleness role; (f) honour `[[possibility-probability-slippage]]` — the old figure functioned as evidential garnish for the cognitive-gap claim; the revised figure should not be allowed to slip in the opposite direction (lower similarity does *not* prove the gap is dualistic; it just removes one popular objection); (g) audit for any *other* articles in `topics/`, `concepts/`, `apex/`, or `voids/` that cite the same figure (grep for "98%", "99%", "share.*DNA", "DNA.*share" — three additional matches in `experimental-consciousness-science-2025-2026.md`, `decoherence-and-macroscopic-superposition.md`, and `voids/resolution-void.md` per initial grep, though those may be unrelated false positives). Short-medium scope (~150-300 words touched across two articles plus citations). Tenet alignment: methodological (current-literature fidelity; evidential-status-discipline as anti-staleness pass). See `topics/animal-consciousness.md:110` and `apex/minds-without-words.md:78`.
