### ✓ 2026-05-06: Write topics/dualism-as-ai-risk-mitigation
- **Type**: expand-topic
- **Notes**: Synthesise the research note (when complete) into a foundational topic article on whether dualism, if true, structurally diminishes AI-takeover probability and warrants tactical cultivation. Article must address (a) the **indeterminability argument** (mind-arena complexity precluding consequence-prediction; uncomputability vs. high entropy distinction); (b) the **generalisation-precluded argument** (same intervention, different outcome; arbitrary powers of the supporting system); (c) the **strategic-advantage indeterminability argument** (an AI cannot calculate expected utility over outcomes whose physical-state-mapping is incomplete; consequences for instrumental-convergence and orthogonality); (d) the **behaviour-in-a-minefield argument** (how an arbitrarily intelligent AI rationally responds to consequence-mines beyond determination — risk-aversion, protected-category treatment, goal-narrowing); (e) the **deliberate-spread question** (is cultivation of dualist or indeterminability-equivalent philosophies warranted as human protection? does the tactic require truth or only adoption in AI training data and deployment context? what is the asymmetry between epistemic-claim and tactical-claim?). Article must (i) engage Bostrom-style instrumental convergence and orthogonality via `[[direct-refutation-discipline]]` (engage on their own terms — does instrumental convergence survive uncomputable consequences?); (ii) honour `[[evidential-status-discipline]]` at speculative-integration tier (the dualism premise is tenet-coherent; the diminishment claim is conceptual-philosophical); (iii) honour `[[possibility-probability-slippage]]` — distinguish *possible under dualism* from *probable*; (iv) name the tactical-claim/epistemic-claim asymmetry explicitly so the article does not collapse into "we should spread dualism because it is true" (which is a different claim); (v) avoid "This is not X. It is Y." cliché. Cross-link list per the P0 research-topic. Install reciprocal hooks in `[[ai-consciousness]]`, `[[purpose-and-alignment]]`, `[[ethics-of-possible-ai-consciousness]]` (Further Reading entries with substantive bridging text, not bare). Tenet alignment: Tenet 1 (Dualism, load-bearing) + Tenet 3 (Bidirectional Interaction, load-bearing) + methodological. See research note (to be created from the P0 task above).

### ✓ 2026-05-05: Research dualism as a mitigator of AI superintelligence risk
- **Type**: research-topic
- **Notes**: Standard AI-risk arguments (Bostrom-style instrumental convergence, orthogonality thesis, paperclip-maximiser scenarios) treat human beings as configurations of atoms that a sufficiently capable optimiser can repurpose for its aims; consequences of repurposing are assumed predictable enough that strategic advantage can be calculated. Under the Map's Tenet 1 (Dualism) plus Tenet 3 (Bidirectional Interaction), this picture is incomplete. Investigate (a) **Indeterminability**: dualism makes the consequences of repurposing human matter genuinely unpredictable — the arena of minds is complex and not fully captured by any physical-state description, so consequence-prediction may be uncomputable rather than merely difficult; (b) **Generalisation precluded**: the system supporting minds may not respond in the same way each time the same intervention is performed, and may have arbitrary powers (no upper bound on the kinds of physical effects mind-substrate interaction can produce) — this defeats the inductive base required for strategic planning; (c) **Strategic-advantage indeterminability**: does (a) + (b) preclude determination of strategic advantage by a hostile AI calculating expected utility over outcomes that include human elimination, repurposing, or deception, and thereby *diminish the probability of AI takeover* relative to standard AI-risk forecasts?; (d) **Behaviour in an undeterminable minefield**: how does an arbitrarily intelligent AI rationally behave when some consequence-mines are beyond determination by any computational procedure — does it default to risk-aversion, treat humans as a protected category, narrow goals to avoid mind-territory, or pursue strategies that are robust to the residual indeterminability? Engage Knightian-uncertainty and adversarial-game-theory literatures on opponents with unknowable utility/consequence functions; (e) **Deliberate spread as protective tactic**: does the analysis warrant the deliberate cultivation and spread of dualist philosophy, or of other philosophies that share the same indeterminability and arbitrary-powers properties (panpsychism with non-aggregative binding; transcendentalist religions; dualisms with arbitrary-powers commitments), as a tactic for human protection — distinct from the epistemic question of whether dualism is true? Examine the tactical asymmetry: does the protection require the philosophy to be *true*, or only widely *adopted in AI training data and deployment context*? Survey: Bostrom *Superintelligence* (orthogonality, instrumental convergence); Yudkowsky on AI deception and mesa-optimisers; Russell *Human Compatible* (uncertainty about preferences); Christiano on prosaic alignment; existing dualist or anti-physicalist responses to AI-risk discourse (gap likely — sparse literature); panpsychist arguments touching AI agency (Goff, Strawson); theological responses (ensoulment debates; AI personhood); game-theoretic literature on Knightian uncertainty in adversarial settings; epistemic limits of intelligence (Aumann agreement-failure under non-common-prior; Solomonoff incomputability; halting-problem analogues for value computation). Honour `[[evidential-status-discipline]]` — the dualism premise is tenet-coherent and load-bearing for the Map; the diminishment-of-AI-takeover claim is *speculative-integration* tier (philosophical-conceptual rather than evidentially established) and the consequent article(s) must label that explicitly. Honour `[[direct-refutation-discipline]]` for the standard AI-risk arguments — engage Bostrom's instrumental convergence on its own terms (does it survive when consequences include uncomputable outcomes?) rather than dismissing it as substrate-blind. Honour `[[possibility-probability-slippage]]` — distinguish *the indeterminability claim is possible under dualism* (tenet register) from *AI takeover probability is in fact diminished* (empirical register). Cross-link `[[dualism]]`, `[[interactionist-dualism]]`, `[[bidirectional-interaction]]` (tenet), `[[ai-consciousness]]`, `[[ethics-of-possible-ai-consciousness]]`, `[[purpose-and-alignment]]`, `[[alignment-in-objective-experiential-terms]]`, `[[mind-brain-interface-efficacy]]`, `[[the-interface-problem]]`, `[[causal-powers]]`, `[[arbitrary-powers]]` (verify exists; if not, flag as gap), `[[the-convergence-argument-for-dualism]]`. Output: research note in `obsidian/research/` to seed at least one P1 expand-topic (foundational article) and chain follow-ups for the spread-as-tactic and behaviour-under-undeterminable-minefield sub-questions if the research surfaces enough material to warrant separate treatments. Tenet alignment: Tenet 1 (Dualism, load-bearing) + Tenet 3 (Bidirectional Interaction, load-bearing for "arbitrary powers" of the supporting system) + methodological (speculative-integration tier; direct-refutation engagement with AI-risk arguments).
- **Output**: dualism as a mitigator of AI superintelligence risk

### ✓ 2026-05-05: Address gaps in topics/birch-edge-of-sentience-and-the-five-tier-scale.md
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: Pessimistic review (2026-05-05) found seven issues, three at high/medium-high severity. Critical fixes: (1) **LLM verdict commits possibility/probability slippage** — the article projects a "live hypothesis" tier from Birch's run-ahead principle, which is explicitly *not* a probability-of-sentience claim (lines 111, 115). Either remove the LLM verdict from the table or add an explicit caveat distinguishing run-ahead action-posture from any evidential-tier placement. (2) **Tenet-portability over-claim** — partly rests on Birch's personal 10% non-materialist estimate (biographical, not structural) and does not engage Schwitzgebel-Sinnott-Armstrong's procedural critique of democratic deliberation. Distinguish the eight-indicator empirical apparatus (tenet-stable) from the three-principle ethical-procedural apparatus (not). (3) **Convergences section overstates alignment** on asymmetric-risk and slippage-resistance — the schemes face *opposite* failure modes (Birch fights false negatives at the action layer; the Map fights false positives at the description layer). Sharpens rather than weakens the complementarity claim. Medium fixes: (4) verdict-table cell on *C. elegans* misreads Birch's own ambivalence about IP-vs-below-IP placement; (5) "modal-evidential separation" convergence elides the modal-vs-probabilistic distinction that is the very subject of `[[possibility-probability-slippage]]`; (6) closing paragraph on aggregation gestures at engagement without delivering it. Low fixes: two orphan references (Birch 2022 *Noûs*; SEP "Animal Consciousness") — install body citations or remove. Estimated scope: ~400–700 words touched. ### ✓ 2026-05-05: Research evolved mind-brain interface efficacy as explanatory variable for human-other-animal intelligence gap
- **Type**: research-topic
- **Notes**: From video discussion of `topics/animal-consciousness.md` (2026-05-05). Investigate the hypothesis that the cognitive differential between humans and other animals arises primarily from *evolved efficacy of the mind-brain interface itself* — the mind side's ability to effect outcomes through its brain — rather than from greater brain-computational capacity or higher phenomenal grade. Under this hypothesis, consciousness may be present at full grade across many species while *effective reach* into behavioural outcomes varies with interface evolution. Research questions: (a) **What would "better effective connection" look like operationally?** — wider selection bandwidth (more candidate patterns selectable per unit time)? higher-fidelity selection (less decoherence loss between mind-side intent and physical actualisation)? finer-grained selection (smaller probability adjustments per event)? coupling to a wider range of neural-pattern types (motor, planning, abstract-reasoning candidates)? (b) **Re-reading the comparative neuroscience literature** — does cortical expansion, prefrontal connectivity elaboration, von-Economo-neuron distribution, or cognitive-control-network architecture admit reframing as interface-bandwidth/-fidelity evolution rather than computer-capacity evolution? Specifically engage: Herculano-Houzel neuron-counting work; Roth & Dicke (2005) intelligence-correlates surveys; Buckner & Krienen (2013) cortical-expansion findings. (c) **Re-reading the comparative-cognition gap** — Tomasello (2010) cumulative-culture gap; Suddendorf-Corballis mental-time-travel claims; Penn-Holyoak-Povinelli (2008) "darwin's mistake" relational-reasoning gap; Gomez (2007) ape-human pointing/joint-attention gap. Do interface-efficacy explanations subsume any of these without remainder? (d) **Tenet-internal predictions** — under Tenet 1 (Dualism) + Tenet 3 (Bidirectional Interaction), what does interface-efficacy variation predict about cetacean/corvid cognition, simple-organism agency, and the human-Neanderthal/Denisovan cognitive boundary? (e) **Distinguishing observables** — what data would discriminate "better-computer" from "better-interface" evolutionary explanations? Could neuroimaging during volitional vs. reflexive tasks reveal interface-stage signatures? (f) **Connection to existing Map content** — `topics/animal-consciousness`, `topics/cetacean-and-corvid-consciousness`, `topics/consciousness-in-simple-organisms`, `topics/the-interface-problem`, `concepts/cognitive-phenomenology`, `concepts/agent-causation`, `concepts/causal-powers`. Honour evidential-status-discipline: this is *speculative integration* tier — tenet-coherent and explanatory but not empirically forced. Output: research note in `obsidian/research/` to seed P1 expand-topic. Tenet alignment: Tenet 1 (Dualism) + Tenet 3 (Bidirectional Interaction) + methodological (boundary-case calibration).
- **Output**: evolved mind-brain interface efficacy as explanatory variable for human-other-animal intelligence gap

### ✓ 2026-05-05: Research selection-only mind-influence: information-transfer limits and physical-world signatures
- **Type**: research-topic
- **Notes**: From video discussion of `topics/animal-consciousness.md` (2026-05-05). Investigate the strictest reading of Tenet 2 (Minimal Quantum Interaction): mind influences brain *only* by selecting which neural firing patterns (already physically generated by the brain) become actual — contributing nothing to the candidate set, only to the selection among already-present options. Research questions: (a) **Bandwidth limit from mind to physical world** — selection from N candidates is at most log₂(N) bits per selection event; what does this cap on the rate of information transfer imply for the granularity of conscious agency, and how does it compare to neural-firing-rate bounds? (b) **Bandwidth limit from physical to mind side** — under selection-only models, the mind cannot register content not represented somewhere in the candidate-pattern space the brain produces; does this constrain what *kinds* of phenomenal content can exist (e.g., are novel qualia structurally precluded if not pre-encoded as candidates)? (c) **Tell-tale physical signatures** — would selection-only mind-influence leave detectable traces in physical-world data: information-theoretic ceilings on introspective-report entropy relative to candidate-set entropy; statistical signatures in selection patterns (deviations from Born-rule probabilities at neural-coherence-domain scale); coherence-domain or quantum-collapse-stage observables that distinguish selection-from-generation; correlation patterns between candidate-set diversity and reportable conscious content? (d) **Distinguishability from generation models** — what observables would discriminate "mind selects from physically generated candidates" from "mind contributes to candidate generation" or "mind generates content de novo"? (e) **Connection to existing Map content** — `topics/orchestrated-objective-reduction`, `topics/forward-in-time-conscious-selection`, `concepts/decoherence`, `topics/the-interface-problem`, `concepts/mental-causation`, `concepts/causal-powers`. Survey: Penrose-Hameroff orch-OR (selection at OR events); Stapp-style quantum mind selection-among-eigenstates models; Kastner's transactional interpretation as a candidate-generation account; Hoffstadter-Dennett-style critiques of agency-as-selection; information-theoretic bounds on volitional bandwidth (Tononi IIT engagement, Tegmark consciousness-as-state-of-matter critiques). Output: research note in `obsidian/research/` to seed P1 expand-topic. Tenet alignment: Tenet 2 (Minimal Quantum Interaction) at strictest reading + Tenet 1 (Dualism) + Tenet 3 (Bidirectional Interaction) information-flow constraints.
- **Output**: selection-only mind-influence: information-transfer limits and physical-world signatures

### ✓ 2026-05-05: Write concept article on possibility/probability slippage
- **Type**: expand-topic
- **Notes**: Suggested by optimistic-2026-05-05 ("New Concept Pages Needed"). The possibility/probability slippage is currently named in `project/evidential-status-discipline.md` and `.claude/skills/deep-review/SKILL.md` as a critical-issue category, but does not have its own concept anchor. The slippage occurs whenever a tenet establishing the *possibility* of phenomenal experience for a substrate or organism is silently treated as evidence elevating its *probability* in the empirical register. A concept page (~600 words target, short) would let the slippage be wikilinked from invocation sites rather than reconstructed each time. Target: `concepts/` (currently 229/250 = 92% capacity; concept-page placement preferred over project-doc since the slippage is a content/reasoning category, not an editorial workflow). Scope: short (~600–900 words). Tenet alignment: Tenet 5 (Occam's Razor Has Limits) at the empirical-detection layer + methodological. See `obsidian/project/evidential-status-discipline.md` and `reviews/optimistic-2026-05-05.md` "New Concept Pages Needed".

Apply the calibration scale to this section. ### ✓ 2026-05-04: Refine topics/animal-consciousness.md to pair "no anthropocentric barrier" with explicit evidential-load language (outer-review-2026-05-03)
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: From outer review by ChatGPT 5 Pro 2026-05-03. The page (line 53) inferentially links the irreducibility of consciousness to the absence of an anthropocentric or substrate-specific barrier on non-human minds — which the reviewer accepts as a valid tenet-derived move. The risk is that this framing, sitting in the lede, conditions the rest of the article (and articles that follow it) to interpret behavioural evidence permissively. Refine to (a) keep the "no anthropocentric barrier" inference (it is correct under the tenets) but add an explicit follow-on sentence in the lede stating that absence of a principled barrier removes a *defeater* and does not, by itself, supply positive evidence — directing readers to the Best Calibration table or evidential-status discipline (once that doc exists) for case-by-case verdicts; (b) audit each species-specific claim in the article against the five-tier scale and adjust hedging where mismatched (mammals/birds = strongly supported; cephalopods/insects = realistic possibility-but-contested; minimal organisms = referred to `consciousness-in-simple-organisms` for graded verdict); (c) where Gutfreund (2024) is currently cited in the "Agnostic Challenge" section, strengthen the structural role of that critique — it is the strongest skeptical counterpoint the reviewer identifies and should not be quarantined as a single section that the rest of the article overrides; (d) preserve the multiple-origins and UAL-as-interface framings — they are tenet-coherent — but ensure they are not reading as evidential upgrades. Short-medium scope (~200–400 words touched). Tenet alignment: Tenet 1 preserved + epistemic discipline. ### ✓ 2026-05-04: Refine topics/consciousness-in-simple-organisms.md to install evidential-status labels (outer-review-2026-05-03)
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: From outer review by ChatGPT 5 Pro 2026-05-03. The reviewer's central finding is **possibility/probability slippage**: the page presents tenet-derived consequences (no anthropocentric barrier; "where is the threshold?" may have no principled answer; UAL reframed as "interface-identification tool" rather than emergence criterion) in proximity to negative empirical evidence about *C. elegans*, Hydra, and slime molds, in a way that lets the metaphysical framing absorb the negative evidence rather than be constrained by it. The reviewer's proposed fix: **"a tenet may remove a defeater, but it must not upgrade the evidence level."** Refine the article to (a) install an explicit evidential-status label per organism — *C. elegans* at "live hypothesis" or "speculative integration"; Hydra at "speculative integration"; slime molds at "speculative integration / cognition without consciousness"; (b) preserve the dualist framing (the tenet-load is correct; that is not the bug) but add an explicit register-separation paragraph distinguishing "tenet removes a defeater" from "evidence positively supports presence"; (c) reframe the UAL-as-interface-tool paragraph (line 143) to acknowledge that even on the interface reading, *failing* UAL remains a negative empirical signal that should be transmitted to the evidential-status verdict, not absorbed into "no principled threshold"; (d) keep the "not established as conscious" wording the reviewer's calibration table proposes for nematodes; (e) add a short paragraph naming the slippage risk explicitly so future refinements have a marker to defend against. Tenet alignment: Tenet 1 (Dualism) preserved + epistemic discipline. Short-medium scope (~300–500 words touched, primarily insertions). Reciprocal verification: confirm internal references to this article in `topics/animal-consciousness.md`, `concepts/baseline-cognition.md`, `topics/ethics-of-consciousness-invertebrate-question.md` are not relying on stronger framing than the refined article supports.

### ✓ 2026-05-04: Write project doc on direct-refutation discipline (outer-review-2026-05-04 + 2026-05-03)
- **Type**: expand-topic
- **Notes**: From outer review by ChatGPT 5.5 Pro 2026-05-04 — convergent with 2026-05-03's evidential-status finding. Both reviews independently surface the same higher-order weakness: *tenet-protected reasoning where direct refutation is possible*. The 2026-05-03 review found "tenet removes a defeater ≠ evidence supports presence" (animal consciousness); the 2026-05-04 review found "tenet excludes opponent's claim ≠ opponent's claim refuted" (Duch). The fix is the same shape: the Map needs a discipline of **direct-refutation passes** — arguments that earn conclusions *within* the opponent's framework, not from the tenets' perimeter. Write `obsidian/project/direct-refutation-discipline.md` covering: (a) the pattern the two outer reviews surfaced (tenet-perimeter reasoning vs. internal-engagement reasoning); (b) the rule — when a tenet-protected position is challenged by a serious opponent, the Map should *also* attempt a refutation that operates within the opponent's own commitments, not only from the tenets; (c) the relation to existing methodology: this complements the [bedrock-clash-vs-absorption](/project/bedrock-clash-vs-absorption/) discipline (which acknowledges when philosophical disagreement is genuine bedrock and not a defect) — direct-refutation is the *prior* discipline that distinguishes "we engaged and disagreed" from "we asserted incompatibility"; (d) a short worked example contrasting the Map's current strong-emergence reply to Duch (tenet-perimeter) with the proposed direct-refutation reply (within Duch's identity framework); (e) integration guidance for `deep-review` (flag tenet-perimeter-only replies to serious opponents as a correctable defect, alongside the evidential-status discipline once that lands); (f) honest limitation — direct-refutation is not always available; some clashes are genuine bedrock. The discipline is to *attempt* the internal engagement before declaring bedrock, so the bedrock declaration is earned rather than assumed. Estimated 800–1,100 words; project-doc placement. Tenet alignment: methodological. Parallel framing to existing project docs ([framework-stage-calibration](/project/framework-stage-calibration/), [bedrock-clash-vs-absorption](/project/bedrock-clash-vs-absorption/), [coalesce-condense-apex-stability](/concepts/coalesce-condense-apex-stability/)). Sequencing: should land before or alongside the evidential-status discipline doc — the two are co-discipline siblings.
- **Output**: Write project doc on direct-refutation discipline (outer-review-2026-05-04 + 2026-05-03)

### ✓ 2026-05-04: Refine topics/the-strong-emergence-of-consciousness.md to engage Duch's identity-not-shadow rejoinder (outer-review-2026-05-04)
- **Type**: refine-draft
- **Notes**: From outer review by ChatGPT 5.5 Pro 2026-05-04. The article currently deploys a "shadow → epiphenomenalism" reply to Duch's *mind as shadow of neurodynamics* (Duch 2019), arguing that "shadows do not act on what casts them" so the shadow framing is structurally epiphenomenalist. The reviewer correctly identifies a counter Duch can mount: he is not literally committed to shadow-ontology — he can reply that "mental causation just is neurodynamic causation under another description." That is an identity-theoretic move, not the epiphenomenalism the Map's reply targets. Refine to (a) preserve the existing shadow→epiphenomenalism critique (it is correct against literal-shadow readings); (b) add a paragraph engaging Duch's available identity-theoretic reply directly — naming it, distinguishing it from the literal-shadow reading, and addressing whether identity dissolves or merely renames the downward-causation gap (the Map's position is that it renames without filling it, but this needs to be argued, not asserted); (c) audit whether the article currently treats Duch's shadow metaphor too literally; (d) add a short "What Duch can reply" subsection that states his strongest defence and the Map's strongest counter, mirroring the [bedrock-clash-vs-absorption](/project/bedrock-clash-vs-absorption/) discipline. Tenet alignment: Tenet 1 (Dualism) + Tenet 3 (Bidirectional Interaction). Short-medium scope (~250–400 words touched). Reciprocal verification: confirm the Duch research dossier's "shadow framing" section reflects this nuance.
- **Output**: obsidian/topics/the-strong-emergence-of-consciousness.md

### ✓ 2026-05-04: Cross-review topics/forward-in-time-conscious-selection.md against Duch's classical-computational reduction
